<Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
This Robeks is a chill spot. There are a couple of tables and a decent amount of hard chairs. There are usually samples available for customers. In my experience, their customer service is on point. Depending on the direction one is coming from, the store is not simple to access (or see) due to its location. There's not much parking directly in front of the store though a lot of parking within walking distance of the store.

I've come to learn if Robeks (at least this location) has the ingredients to make a recipe that is not (visually) on the menu, they will make it upon request. The Almond Delight is really really tasty. If it's not visible on the menu, ask if the ingredients are available. It's worth learning the recipe to make it myself tasty. Also, registering to be a Robeks member (free) comes with decent perks.< /review>

{'time': 1570218189852, 'text': 'Hi Rosemarie, Natural juices separate due to the fact that fruits and vegetables consist of water and nutrients (all the parts which aren‚Äôt water). For example, Kale is consists of 84% water. So when these fruits and vegetables are juiced, a lot of that nutrient-dense water comes out too. If left to sit, the water is lighter than the vitamins, minerals and all the goodness, which then sinks to the bottom.\nIf the juice has separated then you can be confident that there are no additives. Most store bought drinks don‚Äôt separate because they have chemical stabilizers added to the juice so that it looks perfect in the bottle to the consumer‚Äôs eye.  At Robeks, we only use fresh produce so separation is natural!  Hope this answers your feedback.  If you have any further feedback or questions about our juices, please feel free to leave your feedback at http://robeks.com/connect/contact-us.html where we can actually have someone directly get in touch to explain ingredients!  Sincerely, Robeks'}</Response>

<user_name>Remington le<//user_name><Time>1618374743494< /Time><Rating>4<//Rating>< text>
Went today to have something mala with one other person.  We ordered the cucumber salad, intestine dry pot, Kangxi noodles (grandmas spicy noodles?), and rice.

Their portions are huge, and the prices are very fair for what you get.  The Kangxi noodles were numbing spicy, with salty bits of pork and savory peanuts. The intestine dry pot had soft tender potatoes, chewy and sometimes soft intestines (wished there was more tender pieces, but some parts of the intestines are just chewier) , and cauliflower carrying a lot of the flavors from the sauce.  The cucumber salad was cool and refreshing, and great to have in between bites.

We couldn‚Äôt finish any of the dishes in one sitting, the leftovers are going to last for at least another day‚Äôs worth of meals. Will definitely come back to try other things on the menu, I‚Äôm a fan.

________________________________
Some of the lowest scoring reviews are a little crazy:
the food is going to have lots of oil that is spicy, it wouldn‚Äôt be authentic otherwise.
I don‚Äôt understand why I would care about masks being held up by double sided tape if the food from the kitchen was some of the best offered in the area.
If someone‚Äôs going to ban you from their restaurant, it‚Äôs probably just not because you called their cake dry.

UTA is United Taiwanese Association.  It‚Äôs maybe a club from UCSD?< /text>

< review>
We decided to try this Chinese restaurant for the first time. I guess that it had a different restaurant name before a change of ownership
We had a nice experience here and the food was nicely prepared. The service was nice and our server, although a little quiet, was still friendly, helpful, and informative about the menu. The restaurant is spacious and has a nice decor.

We decided to order four dishes. The dry fried string beans were great and had a great flavor. We have had the same dish in other restaurants but this one was really good. The second dish we ordered was a spicy squid with peppers. It was delicious and did not have a fishy smell. Our main dish my partner and I ordered soup dishes. I will say the portion if soup you get is quite large and very filling. I ordered the Beef Noodles Soup. The broth was great and had lots of noodles and beef. The beef itself was tender. My partner had the Kangxi Spicy Noodle. It was great and yes quite spicy.

Overall we had a nice experience and would return to try some dishes from Northern China. Our service was nice and so was the food.< /review>

< Review>
Good food, tasty dishes. The menu is a combo of Dongbei (Northeastern China) food, Sichuan, and Hunan food. The latter two offer spicy dishes, Dongbei food is not spicy, with more meaty and hearty dishes.

Friendly services, fast and attentive. A good Chinese food selection on Convoy.< /Review>

< text>
This is one of my favorite Chinese restaurant in San Diego. I went there with UTA (the taiwanese org) in the very first time, and in love with it. They served Sichuan cuisine which is known for their spiciness. and all their dishes we ordered were on point. We ordered Spicy grilled whole fish and sliced pork with green pepper which are both their signatures. you could tell that the fish is fresh, the pork is not overcooked, even their sauce is perfect. all their dishes were all in quite big portion, so it's good that we can take away some of it and save the money for the next meal! The place is quite big, clean and the service was good and very attentive. This is defitnitely my go-to Asian restaurant. I recommend to all of you.<//text>

<userid>102053839186264460915<//userid>< Name>
Tim Lowery< /Name>
< Time>
1560789009481< /Time>
<rate>5<//rate>< review>
Excellent Hunan cuisine and great service! Hunan food has the reputation for being extremely spicy which puts a lot of people off. However, there are definitely milder more accessible dishes available in this cuisine for those like me who can't take extreme heat. On my visit yesterday I had three dishes. The first was the northern crispy pork, crispy fried slices of pork with a crisp batter and glazed with a tangy sweet and sour sauce. Very tasty! Next a stir fry of tender beef with white and green onions, very well prepared. The high point was the braised whole fish served in a nicely seasoned sauce and topped with tofu, baby bok choy, and cilantro. This was absolutely delicious!

The staff is very friendly and helpful. I highly recommend this place! I'll definitely be back soon.<//review>

< Text>
I have long been of fan of Stamper Family Optometry and now more than ever. I'm so happy I found Dr. David of the Stamper Clan. ( Three generations of eye docs in this office since 1913. ) After wearing hard contact lenses since age twelve other doctors told me I'd never be able to wear soft lenses. Dr. David, as opposed to his Uncle, Dr. Bruce (called by their first names to avoid the confusion of having two Doctor Stampers in the same office, ) suggested I take a lens holiday. After six months of only wearing glasses I returned and Dr. David was surprised but excited that my corneas looked nearly normal. Decades of polymer plastic lenses do tend to reshape the eye. Mine bounced back like memory foam! Next we discussed my options. Bi-focal glasses? No. Contacts and reading glasses?  No. What about monocular vision? I dunno. He explained and said it wasn't for everyone but I said I was willing to give it a try.

First he determined my dominate eye. This is the eye you use when looking through the viewfinder on a camera or a rifle for that matter. It usually corresponds to your dexterity. He then fitted my dominant left eye for distance vision. Then my right eye was fitted for close-up. He said some people know within an hour if they can do it or not. I was required to stay on the premises for an hour in the event I was one of those people who get nauseous or dizzy. I must say at first the concept alone almost made me cross-eyed but now I think of it as the Poor Man's Lasik Surgery. I could read the clock on a building a block away, I could read the tiny print in a text message and was relieved I didn't have to fumble about for my "reading glasses" to wear over my contacts like I had been doing for way too long.

I was hooked in the first fifteen minutes. No integration issues for my brain!  I don't miss seeing things in stereo, in fact my sight seems to be the best it's ever been and the contacts feel like a dream compared to the old school blind child hard lenses I endured for decades. Dr. David s a great find, he specializes in the "hard to fit" eye. The multi-lingual staff is another big plus. Jhosy got me up to speed on soft lens insertion and removal including a special tip for us "long-nailed" girls. Sweet Esmerelda gave me the visual  test; while Jose was busy tightening my sunglasses that were slipping down my nose but took it a step further and replaced the screw! Sixteen employees, some there ten to twenty years, multi-tasking with the synchronicity of a Swiss watch in their daily routine. The customer service and commitment to the patient's satisfaction is outstanding!</Text>

<Time>1516508613759</Time>< Review>
Excellent service and extremely good food. Ordered the parihuela peruana... Seafood soup.  I asked for it to be not spicy for my toddler, and it came a little bit spicy the first time. When my server (Oskar) checked on me and saw that we were not eating it he proactively changed it for me to a non spicy one, and it was delicious! The mussels were really good and the fish in there and shrimp were also good. Only thing is octopus in there was chewy. Side of garlic bread was finger licking good. My toddler ate it all up super fast (minus the octopus). And she's a foodie. So when she eats it I know the food is very high quality. Also ordered a side of vegetables which came as cauliflower, broccoli and carrots cut very tiny, sauteed with salt and butter. Delicious as well. Especially when I put it in the soup to eat together. Overall great experience. Would definitely come back and try the other dishes!

Second time here and continue to be impressed. Ordered the:
*Red snapper... Wow. Perfectly cooked. Will order again
*Churrasco.. good. Prefer the fish.
*Our favorite side veggie.. still awesome!
Even had some live music tonight!  Single guitar player.</Review>

< text>
Pretty average place to eat.  The most anyone part of the breakfast was the waitresses.  One came to get my drink order (water) and didn't bring it.  Someone else asked me and brought it maybe 10 minutes later.  When the rest of our party came in, we ordered their drinks and again she forgot.  And she even got the drink order wrong (one iced tea, one water extra lemon and a Coke with a water).  Not terribly difficult.  When she did refill the drinks there was no ice so all the water was warm.  We even had to repeat the dessert order when standing right in front of her and it was only 2 tiny cupcakes.  They weren't even busy there was only two other tables occupied.  The food was very average, nothing terribly good not bad.  I've been to both locations and I would say Gilroy is definitely better.</text>

We've been coming here since we moved to MH on Feb of this year--- it's practically across the street from our house. One thing I can say though, very friendly.
